-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-
~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~Introduction-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~
-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-

The world of Dragon Quest IX contains many monsters, and this list here will
be your guide to all of them.

-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-
~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-( Full List By Number )-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~
-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-

This list provides comprehensive data on all monsters in the game.  Each
monster data card contains useful information and is explained further to help
you better understand the data.

You will notice that a few monsters have letters next to their names (such as
the Slime having #001a, #001b, and #001c).  This is to differentiate between
the different variations that appear.

The following statistics are provided on each card:

 EXP - The experience points your party will gain when killing this monster.
Gold - The gold your party will gain when killing this monster.
 ATK - The attack power of the monster.
 DEF - The defense power of the monster.
 AGI - The agility of the monster that also affects its speed.

The monster data card also contains information on the strengths and weaknesses
of the particular monster.  They are divided into Elemental and Status Effects.

Elemental Attributes
 Fire - Fire attribute (Frizz, Frizzle, etc)
  Ice - Ice attribute (Crack, Crackle, etc)
 Wind - Wind attribute (Woosh, Swoosh, etc)
Blast - Explosion and thunder attribute (Bang, Boom, etc)
Earth - Earth attribute (Funereal fource, etc)
 Dark - Dark attribute (Zam, Zammle, etc)
Light - Light attribute (Starburst throw, Life fource, etc)

Status Attributes
Dazle - Hallucinate/Illusion effect
Sleep - Sleep effect
Death - Instant death effect
DrnMP - Drain MP effect
Confu - Confusion effect
Fizle - Block spellcasting effect
 Stop - Stop action effect
Poisn - Poison effect
Prlyz - Paralyze effect
DecAK - Decrease attack effect
DecDF - Decrease defense effect
DecSP - Decrease speed effect
DecMR - Decrease magic resistance effect
Msmrz - Susceptibility to become mesmerized by character's style

Each monster has a value given for each of these attributes.  A higher number
in a given attribute represents a weakness towards that attribute.  A lower
number represents strength and resistance towards that attribute.  Neutral is
defined by the value of 100.  Values above 100 indicate weakness while values
below 100 indicate strength.  A value of zero (0) indicates immunity to that
attribute.

If a monster has Fire at 75 and Ice at 150, it would only take 75% damage from
fire based attacks, but 150% damage from ice based attacks.

The numbers for the Status Attributes indicate how likely that particular
status is to affect the monster when cast upon it.  So you are not very likely
to put a monster to sleep that has the Sleep status attribute at 25.

The percentages next to the item drops represent the percentage chance you have
of acquiring that item at the end of a battle.

-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-
~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~( Legacy Boss Info )-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-[BST05]
-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-

Legacy bosses are bosses that were found in previous Dragon Quest and Dragon
Warrior games.  Dragon Quest 9's post-game content allows you a chance to fight
these bosses and gain some very powerful and interesting items.  They are also
the only place where you can get the coloured orb items, that are required to
create some of the most powerful equipment through alchemy.

Legacy bosses have a neat aspect in that everytime you beat them, you have a
choice to level them up or leave them at the current level that they are.  The
first time you fight them they start at level 1, and can go up to level 99.
As they level up, they not only get stronger, but their item and equipment
can change, and also the rates at which they drop.

These tables below outline the items and equipment that they drop and what the
drop rates are at the various levels.

You will notice the table mentioned "Second Drop" and "Third Drop", but not
"First Drop".  This is because the first drop for ALL legacy bosses is a
mini-medal, and it always has a 100% drop rate.  This means that everytime you
fight a legacy boss and win, you WILL acquire a mini-medal.  Aside from that,
you have a chance to acquire either or both of the second and third drops.


             o---------------------------------------------------o
            /                Legacy Boss: Baramos                 \
           o-------------------------------------------------------o
          /  Level  |    Second Drop     |  %  |  Third Drop  |  %  \
         o-----------------------------------------------------------o
         |   1 - 3  |   Aliahan Boots    | 20% |  Silver Orb  |  5%  |
         |   4 - 8  |   Aliahan Boots    | 25% |  Silver Orb  |  5%  |
         |   9 - 15 |  Aliahan Clothes   | 20% |  Silver Orb  |  6%  |
         |  16 - 25 |    Murdaw's Map    | 10% |  Silver Orb  |  6%  |
         |  26 - 40 |    Murdaw's Map    | 15% |  Silver Orb  |  7%  |
         |  41 - 56 |    Murdaw's Map    | 20% |  Silver Orb  |  7%  |
         |  57 - 68 |    Murdaw's Map    | 25% |  Silver Orb  |  8%  |
         |  69 - 80 |    Murdaw's Map    | 30% |  Silver Orb  |  8%  |
         o  81 - 90 |    Murdaw's Map    | 35% |  Silver Orb  |  9%  o
          \ 91 - 99 |    Murdaw's Map    | 40% |  Silver Orb  | 10% /
           o-------------------------------------------------------o

             o---------------------------------------------------o
            /                Legacy Boss: Murdaw                  \
           o-------------------------------------------------------o
          /  Level  |    Second Drop     |  %  |  Third Drop  |  %  \
         o-----------------------------------------------------------o
         |   1 - 3  |    Somnia Boots    | 20% |  Yellow Orb  |  5%  |
         |   4 - 8  |    Somnia Boots    | 25% |  Yellow Orb  |  5%  |
         |   9 - 15 |   Somnia Clothes   | 15% |  Yellow Orb  |  6%  |
         |  16 - 25 |  Dhoulmagus' Map   | 10% |  Yellow Orb  |  6%  |
         |  26 - 40 |  Dhoulmagus' Map   | 15% |  Yellow Orb  |  7%  |
         |  41 - 56 |  Dhoulmagus' Map   | 20% |  Yellow Orb  |  7%  |
         |  57 - 68 |  Dhoulmagus' Map   | 25% |  Yellow Orb  |  8%  |

~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~( Top Ten Monsters )-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~
-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-

~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~( Pre-Game )~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~[BST06]

The two tables here are the top 10 monsters for Exp and Gold found before you
finish the game (pre-game).  They specifically DO NOT include any monsters that
are exclusively found in Grottos (treasure map dungeons), due to the fact that
most of those dungeons are only accessible post-game (after you finish the
game).

                 |   2  | Metal medley       | 12288 |   60  |

                 |   4  | Metal slime        |  4096 |   20  |
                 |   5  | Great troll        |  3800 |   78  |

                 |   7  | Drakulard          |  3450 |  152  |
                 |   8  | Barbatos           |  3400 |  187  |
                 o   9  | Firn fiend         |  3200 |  172  o
                  \  10 | Gigantes           |  3200 |  110 /

-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-
~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-( Grotto Monsters )-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-[BST07]
-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-~-

In the treasure map dungeons (grottos), you will fight a host of different
monsters.  The maps you will get will create a dungeon that is one of five
types: Nature, Ruins, Ice, Volcano and Water.  The atmosphere of each type of
dungeon obviously changes, but also the monsters within change.  Dungeons are
also given a level ranking which determines how difficult that dungeon is.
This level ranking determines the number of floors, the types of loot in the
chests, and the overall difficulty.  For our purposes right now, this level
ranking also determines the Rank that each floor in the dungeon will be.  The
Rank of a floor is a letter that starts at K (weakest), and goes backwards all
the way to A (strongest), with the very strongest being S rank.  As you
progress down the floors of a dungeon, the Rank of the floors will increase.

Depending on the Rank of the floor and the type of dungeon that you are in,
the monsters that you will encounter are set.  The tables below outline the
different types of monsters you will find together.  If you are looking for
a specific monster (for example, Moai minstrel for the Luminary quest), then
try to get dungeon maps that are of a higher level, so that the floor Ranks
can be higher.


      o-----------------------------------------------------------------o
     /                              Nature                               \
    o---------------------------------------------------------------------o
   / Rank |                       Monsters Found                           \
  o-------------------------------------------------------------------------o
  |   K   | Mushroom mage, Chimaera, Dread admiral, Big badboon,            |
  |       | Purrestidigitator, Crabid                                       |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   J   | Bewarewolf, Pink sanguini, Mandrake major, Scourgette,          |
  |       | Drackal, Treeface                                               |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   I   | Crabber dabber doo, Treevil, Peckerel, Brainy badboon,          |
  |       | Sluggernaut, Drackal                                            |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   H   | Swinoceros, Drakularge, Cyclops, Bomboulder,                    |
  |       | Live lava, Tearwolf                                             |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   G   | Splatterhorn, Terrorhawk, Cumulus rex, Gloomy gastropog,        |
  |       | Boss troll, Drakularge                                          |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   F   | Green dragon, Freezing fog, Blastoad, Claws,                    |
  |       | Mandrake marshal, Magmalice                                     |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   E   | Mandrake marshal, Cumulus vex, Cobra cardinal, King cureslime,  |
  |       | Gem jamboree, Red dragon                                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   D   | King crab, Genie sanguini, Prism peacock, Terror troll,         |
  |       | Moai minstrel, Drakulard                                        |
  |-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
  |   C   | Drakulard, Sluggerslaught, Terror troll, Cosmic chimaera,       |
